<h2 id="anatomy" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Anatomy</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">To set up the JSON tree view correctly, you&#x27;ll need to understand its anatomy and how we name its parts.</p>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Each part includes a <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">data-part</code> attribute to help identify them in the DOM.</p>
</blockquote>

<h2 id="examples" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#examples"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Examples</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Learn how to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">JsonTreeView</code> component in your project. Let&#x27;s take a look at the most basic example:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_8fhanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="different-data-types" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#different-data-types"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Different Data Types</h3>

<h3 id="controlling-expand-level" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#controlling-expand-level"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Controlling Expand Level</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">Use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">defaultExpandedDepth</code> prop to control how many levels are expanded by default:</p>

<h3 id="custom-value-rendering" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#custom-value-rendering"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Custom Value Rendering</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">You can customize how specific values are rendered using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">renderValue</code> prop. This example shows how to make email
addresses clickable:</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_9phanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<h3 id="configuration-options" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#configuration-options"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Configuration Options</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The JSON tree view supports several configuration options to customize the display:</p>
<pre class="fs_0.875em lh_1.7142857 mt_1.7142857em mb_1.7142857em bdr_0.375rem p_4 color-scheme_dark [&amp;_code]:bg-c_transparent [&amp;_code]:bd-w_0 [&amp;_code]:bdr_0 [&amp;_code]:p_0 [&amp;_code]:fw_inherit [&amp;_code]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_inherit [&amp;_code]:ff_inherit [&amp;_code]:lh_inherit shiki github-dark-default" style="background-color:#0d1117;color:#e6edf3" tabindex="0"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2"><span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">JsonTreeView.Root</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  data</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">data</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  defaultExpandedDepth</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">2</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  quotesOnKeys</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">true</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  showNonenumerable</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">true</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  maxPreviewItems</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">5</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  collapseStringsAfterLength</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">50</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#79C0FF">  groupArraysAfterLength</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#79C0FF">100</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">  &lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">JsonTreeView.Tree</span><span style="color:#79C0FF"> arrow</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">={</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;</span><span style="color:#7EE787">ChevronRightIcon</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span><span style="color:#FF7B72">}</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3"> /&gt;</span></span>
<span class="line"><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&lt;/</span><span style="color:#7EE787">JsonTreeView.Root</span><span style="color:#E6EDF3">&gt;</span></span></code></pre>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600">Configuration Options:</strong></p>
<ul class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em ps_1.625em li-t_disc [&amp;_&gt;_li]:ps_0.375em [&amp;_&gt;_li]:[&amp;::marker]:c_fg.subtle [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_p]:mb_0.75em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:first-child]:mt_1.25em [&amp;_&gt;_li_&gt;_p:last-child]:mb_1.25em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mt_0.75em [&amp;_ul,_&amp;_ol]:mb_0.75em">
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">quotesOnKeys</code></strong>: Whether to show quotes around object keys</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">showNonenumerable</code></strong>: Whether to show non-enumerable properties</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">maxPreviewItems</code></strong>: Maximum number of items to show in object/array previews</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">collapseStringsAfterLength</code></strong>: Collapse strings longer than this length</li>
<li class="mt_0.5em mb_0.5em"><strong class="c_var(--colors-prose-bold) fw_600"><code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">groupArraysAfterLength</code></strong>: Group array items when array is longer than this length</li>
</ul>
<h3 id="using-the-root-provider" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#using-the-root-provider"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Using the Root Provider</h3>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component provides a context for the JSON tree view. It accepts the value of the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">useJsonTreeView</code>
hook. You can leverage it to access the component state and methods from outside the JSON tree view.</p>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 not-prose [&amp;_&gt;_.example-preview-scope]:bdr-b_0"><div class="d_flex min-h_32 md:min-h_48 bg_bg.default bdr_lg bd-w_1px w_full ov_hidden not-prose example-preview-scope"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_center jc_center flex_1 p_4 md:p_6 w_full"><div class="example-spinner" role="status" aria-label="Loading example"></div></div></div><div data-scope="collapsible" data-part="root" data-state="closed" dir="ltr" id="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_"><button class="button button--variant_outline button--size_xs bd-c_inherit c_fg.default w_full bdr-t_0 bd-t-w_0 bg_bg.default c_fg.muted fw_medium fs_xs gap_1.5 hover:bg_gray.2 hover:c_fg.default" data-scope="collapsible" data-part="trigger" id="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_:trigger" dir="ltr" type="button" data-state="closed" aria-controls="collapsible:_R_a9hanpfn5tlb_:content" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" class="lucide lucide-code icon icon--size_sm" aria-hidden="true"><path d="m16 18 6-6-6-6"></path><path d="m8 6-6 6 6 6"></path></svg>Show Code</button></div></div>
<blockquote class="mt_1.6em mb_1.6em ps_1em fw_500 font-style_italic bd-s-w_0.25rem bd-c_var(--colors-prose-quote-border)">
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">If you&#x27;re using the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">RootProvider</code> component, you don&#x27;t need to use the <code class="c_var(--colors-prose-code) fw_600 bd-w_1px fs_0.875em p_0.125em_0.25em bdr_0.25em bg-c_gray.a2">Root</code> component.</p>
</blockquote>
<h2 id="api-reference" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#api-reference"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>API Reference</h2>

<h2 id="accessibility" class="fs_1.5em mt_2em mb_1em lh_1.3333333 fw_700 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_800 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.875em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Accessibility</h2>
<p class="mt_1.25em mb_1.25em c_var(--colors-prose-body) [&amp;_a]:td_underline [&amp;_a]:fw_500">The JSON tree view is built on top of the Tree View component and complies with the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/treeview/" class="link">Tree View WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-support" class="fs_1.25em lh_1.6 mt_1.6em mb_0.6em fw_600 c_var(--colors-prose-heading) [&amp;_strong]:fw_700 [&amp;_strong]:c_inherit [&amp;_code]:fs_0.9em [&amp;_+_*]:mt_0"><a class="link subheading-anchor" aria-label="Link to section" href="#keyboard-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a>Keyboard Support</h3>
<div class="bd-w_1px bdr_lg ov-x_auto not-prose"><table class="bd_0 table__root table__root--size_sm table__root--variant_outline"><thead class="table__head table__head--size_sm table__head--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Key</th><th class="px_4 bg_gray.2 h_10 table__header table__header--size_sm table__header--variant_outline">Description</th></tr></thead><tbody class="table__body table__body--size_sm table__body--variant_outline"><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Tab</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the tree view, placing the first tree view item in focus.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Enter</kbd><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Space</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Selects the item or branch node</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowDown</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the next node</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowUp</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the previous node</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowRight</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">When focus is on a closed branch node, opens the branch.<br> When focus is on an open branch node, moves focus to the first item node.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">ArrowLeft</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">When focus is on an open branch node, closes the node.<br> When focus is on an item or branch node, moves focus to its parent branch node.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Home</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to first node without opening or closing a node.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">End</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to the last node that can be focused without expanding any nodes that are closed.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">a-z</kbd><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">A-Z</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Focus moves to the next node with a name that starts with the typed character. The search logic ignores nodes that are descendants of closed branch.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">*</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Expands all sibling nodes that are at the same depth as the focused node.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Shift + ArrowDown</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to and toggles the selection state of the next node.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Shift + ArrowUp</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Moves focus to and toggles the selection state of the previous node.</td></tr><tr class="table__row table__row--size_sm table__row--variant_outline"><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_1 flex-d_row"><kbd class="kbd kbd--size_sm c_gray.a11 px_1">Ctrl + A</kbd></div></td><td class="px_4 py_2 table__cell table__cell--size_sm table__cell--variant_outline">Selects all nodes in the tree. If all nodes are selected, unselects all nodes.</td></tr></tbody></table></div></article><div class="d_flex flex-d_column-reverse sm:flex-d_row jc_space-between gap_3"><a class="bdr_lg bd-w_1px d_flex /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nTo set up the JSON tree view correctly, you'll need to understand its anatomy and how we name its parts.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"tree-view\" /\u003e\n\n## Examples\n\nLearn how to use the `JsonTreeView` component in your project. Let's take a look at the most basic example:\n\n**Example: basic**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from and special values:\n\n**Example: array-data**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst testArray = [1, 2, 3, 4, 5]\nObject.defineProperties(testArray, {\n  customProperty: { value: 'custom value', enumerable: false, writable: false },\n  anotherProperty: { value: 42, enumerable: false, writable: false },\n})\n\nexport const ArrayData = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n      defaultExpandedDepth={1}\n      className={styles.Root}\n      data={{\n        normalArray: [1, 2, 3],\n        arrayWithNonEnumerableProperties: testArray,\n        sparseArray: (() =\u003e {\n          const sparse = []\n          sparse[0] = 'first'\n          sparse[5] = 'sixth'\n          return sparse\n        })(),\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree className={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/solid/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from JSON tree:\n\n**Example: functions**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst data = [\n  function sum(a: number, b: number) {\n    return a + b\n  },\n  async (promises: Promise\u003cany\u003e[]) =\u003e await Promise.all(promises),\n  function* generator(a: number) {\n    while (a \u003e 0) {\n      yield a - 1\n    }\n  },\n]\n\nexport const Functions = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root defaultExpandedDepth={1} className={styles.Root} data={data}\u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree className={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst data = {\n React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst data = new Map\u003cstring, any\u003e([\n      [\n        'taglines',\n        new Set([\n          { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'headless components' },\n          { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'framework agnostic' },\n          { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'accessible by default' },\n        ]),\n      ],\n    ]),\n  ],\n])\n\nexport const MapAndSet = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root defaultExpandedDepth={1} className={styles.Root} data={data}\u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree className={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/solid/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst data = new Map\u003cstring, any\u003e([\n  ['name', 'ark-ui-json-tree'],\n  ['license', 'MIT'],\n  ['elements', new Set(['ark-ui', 123, false, true, null, undefined, 456n])],\n  [\n    'nested',\n    new Map\u003cstring, any\u003e([\n      [\n        'taglines',\n        new Set([\n          { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'headless components' },\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root defaultExpandedDepth={1} class={styles.Root} data={data}\u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree class={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/vue/json-tree-view'\nimport { 'MIT'],\n  ['elements', new Set(['ark-ui', 123, false, true, null, undefined, 456n])],\n  [\n    'nested',\n    new Map\u003cstring, any\u003e([\n      [\n        'taglines',\n        new Set([\n          { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'headless components' },\n          { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'framework agnostic' },\n          { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'accessible by default' },\n        ]),\n      ],\n    ]),\n  ],\n])\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Root :defaultExpandedDepth=\"1\" :class=\"styles.Root\" :data=\"data\"\u003e\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree :class=\"styles.Tree\"\u003e\n      \u003ctemplate #arrow\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/template\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/svelte/json-tree-view'\n  import { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\n  const data = new Map\u003cstring, any\u003e([\n    ['name', 'ark-ui-json-tree'],\n    ['license', 'MIT'],\n    ['elements', new Set(['ark-ui', 123, false, true, null, undefined, 456n])],\n    [\n      'nested',\n      new Map\u003cstring, any\u003e([\n        [\n          'taglines',\n          new Set([\n            { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'headless components' },\n            { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'framework agnostic' },\n            { name: 'ark-ui', feature: 'accessible by default' },\n          ]),\n        ],\n      ]),\n    ],\n  ])\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cJsonTreeView.Root defaultExpandedDepth={1} class={styles.Root} {data}\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree class={styles.Tree}\u003e\n    {#snippet arrow()}\n      \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n\u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Controlling Expand Level\n\nUse the `defaultExpandedDepth` prop to control how many levels are expanded by default:\n\n**Example: expand-level**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nexport const ExpandLevel = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n      className={styles.Root}\n      defaultExpandedDepth={2}\n      data={{\n        name: 'John Doe',\n        age: 30,\n        email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n        tags: ['tag1', 'tag2', 'tag3'],\n        address: {\n          street: '123 Main St',\n          city: 'Anytown',\n          state: 'CA',\n          zip: '12345',\n        },\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree className={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/solid/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nexport const ExpandLevel = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n      class={styles.Root}\n      defaultExpandedDepth={2}\n      data={{\n        name: 'John Doe',\n        age: 30,\n        email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n        tags: ['tag1', 'tag2', 'tag3'],\n        address: {\n          street: '123 Main St',\n          city: 'Anytown',\n          state: 'CA',\n          zip: '12345',\n        },\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree class={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/vue/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst data = {\n  name: 'John Doe',\n  age: 30,\n  email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n  tags: ['tag1', 'tag2', 'tag3'],\n  address: {\n    street: '123 Main St',\n    city: 'Anytown',\n    state: 'CA',\n    zip: '12345',\n  },\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :defaultExpandedDepth=\"2\" :data=\"data\"\u003e\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree :class=\"styles.Tree\"\u003e\n      \u003ctemplate #arrow\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/template\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/svelte/json-tree-view'\n  import { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n  class={styles.Root}\n  defaultExpandedDepth={2}\n state: 'CA',\n      zip: '12345',\n    },\n  }}\n\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree class={styles.Tree}\u003e\n    {#snippet arrow()}\n      \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n\u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Custom Value Rendering\n\nYou can customize how specific values are rendered using the `renderValue` prop. This example shows how to make email\naddresses clickable:\n\n**Example: render-value**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nexport const RenderValue = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n      className={styles.Root}\n      defaultExpandedDepth={2}\n      data={{\n        name: 'John Doe',\n        age: 30,\n        number: Number.NaN,\n        email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n        address: {\n          street: '123 Main St',\n          city: 'Anytown',\n          state: 'CA',\n          zip: '12345',\n        },\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree\n        className={styles.Tree}\n        arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e}\n        renderValue={(node) =\u003e {\n          if (node.type === 'text' \u0026\u0026 typeof node.value === 'string' \u0026\u0026 isEmail(node.value)) {\n            return (\n              \u003ca href={`mailto:${node.value}`} target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer\"\u003e\n                {node.value}\n              \u003c/a\u003e\n            )\n          }\n        }}\n      /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst isEmail = (value: string) =\u003e {\n  const strippedValue = value.replace(/^\"(.*)\"$/, '$1')\n  return /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(strippedValue)\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/solid/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nexport const RenderValue = () =\u003e {\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n      class={styles.Root}\n      defaultExpandedDepth={2}\n      data={{\n        name: 'John Doe',\n        age: 30,\n        number: Number.NaN,\n        email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n        address: {\n          street: '123 Main St',\n          city: 'Anytown',\n          state: 'CA',\n          zip: '12345',\n        },\n      }}\n    \u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree\n        class={styles.Tree}\n        arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e}\n        renderValue={(node) =\u003e {\n          if (node.type === 'text' \u0026\u0026 typeof node.value === 'string' \u0026\u0026 isEmail(node.value)) {\n            return (\n              \u003ca href={`mailto:${node.value}`} target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer\"\u003e\n                {node.value}\n              \u003c/a\u003e\n            )\n          }\n        }}\n      /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n  )\n}\n\nconst isEmail = (value: string) =\u003e {\n  const strippedValue = value.replace(/^\"(.*)\"$/, '$1')\n  return /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(strippedValue)\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/vue/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst data = {\n  name: 'John Doe',\n  age: 30,\n  number: Number.NaN,\n  email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n  address: {\n    street: '123 Main St',\n    city: 'Anytown',\n    state: 'CA',\n    zip: '12345',\n  },\n}\n\nconst isEmail = (value: string) =\u003e {\n  const strippedValue = value.replace(/^\"(.*)\"$/, '$1')\n  return /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(strippedValue)\n}\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Root :class=\"styles.Root\" :defaultExpandedDepth=\"2\" :data=\"data\"\u003e\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree :class=\"styles.Tree\"\u003e\n      \u003ctemplate #arrow\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/template\u003e\n      \u003ctemplate #renderValue=\"{ node }\"\u003e\n        \u003ca\n          v-if=\"node.type === 'text' \u0026\u0026 typeof node.value === 'string' \u0026\u0026 isEmail(node.value)\"\n          :href=\"`mailto:${node.value}`\"\n          target=\"_blank\"\n          rel=\"noreferrer\"\n        \u003e\n          {{ node.value }}\n        \u003c/a\u003e\n      \u003c/template\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { JsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/svelte/json-tree-view'\n  import { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\n  const isEmail = (value: string) =\u003e {\n    const strippedValue = value.replace(/^\"(.*)\"$/, '$1')\n    return /^[^\\s@]+@[^\\s@]+\\.[^\\s@]+$/.test(strippedValue)\n  }\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n  class={styles.Root}\n  defaultExpandedDepth={2}\n  data={{\n    name: 'John Doe',\n    age: 30,\n    number: Number.NaN,\n    email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n    address: {\n      street: '123 Main St',\n      city: 'Anytown',\n      state: 'CA',\n      zip: '12345',\n    },\n  }}\n\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree class={styles.Tree}\u003e\n    {#snippet arrow()}\n      \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n    {#snippet renderValue(node)}\n      {#if node.type === 'text' \u0026\u0026 typeof node.value === 'string'}\n        {#if isEmail(node.value)}\n          \u003ca href={`mailto:${node.value}`} target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer\"\u003e\n            {node.value}\n          \u003c/a\u003e\n        {:else}\n          {node.value}\n        {/if}\n      {/if}\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n\u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n\n```\n\n### Configuration Options\n\nThe JSON tree view supports several configuration options to customize the display:\n\n```tsx\n\u003cJsonTreeView.Root\n  data={data}\n  defaultExpandedDepth={2}\n  quotesOnKeys={true}\n  showNonenumerable={true}\n  maxPreviewItems={5}\n  collapseStringsAfterLength={50}\n  groupArraysAfterLength={100}\n\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n\u003c/JsonTreeView.Root\u003e\n```\n\n**Configuration Options:**\n\n- **`quotesOnKeys`**: Whether to show quotes around object keys\n- **`showNonenumerable`**: Whether to show non-enumerable properties\n- **`maxPreviewItems`**: Maximum number of items to show in object/array previews\n- **`collapseStringsAfterLength`**: Collapse strings longer than this length\n- **`groupArraysAfterLength`**: Group array items when array is longer than this length\n\n### Using the Root Provider\n\nThe `RootProvider` component provides a context for the JSON tree view. It accepts the value of the `useJsonTreeView`\nhook. You can leverage it to access the component state and methods from outside the JSON tree view.\n\n**Example: root-provider**\n\n#### React\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView, useJsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/react/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-react'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const jsonTreeView = useJsonTreeView({\n    defaultExpandedDepth: 1,\n    data: {\n      name: 'John Doe',\n      age: 30,\n      email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n      tags: ['tag1', 'tag2', 'tag3'],\n      address: {\n        street: '123 Main St',\n        city: 'Anytown',\n        state: 'CA',\n        zip: '12345',\n      },\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.RootProvider className={styles.Root} value={jsonTreeView}\u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree className={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Solid\n\n```tsx\nimport { JsonTreeView, useJsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/solid/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-solid'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nexport const RootProvider = () =\u003e {\n  const jsonTreeView = useJsonTreeView({\n    defaultExpandedDepth: 1,\n    data: {\n      name: 'John Doe',\n      age: 30,\n      email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n      tags: ['tag1', 'tag2', 'tag3'],\n      address: {\n        street: '123 Main St',\n        city: 'Anytown',\n        state: 'CA',\n        zip: '12345',\n      },\n    },\n  })\n\n  return (\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={jsonTreeView}\u003e\n      \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree class={styles.Tree} arrow={\u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e} /\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.RootProvider\u003e\n  )\n}\n\n```\n\n#### Vue\n\n```vue\n\u003cscript setup lang=\"ts\"\u003e\nimport { JsonTreeView, useJsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/vue/json-tree-view'\nimport { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-vue-next'\nimport styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\nconst jsonTreeView = useJsonTreeView({\n  defaultExpandedDepth: 1,\n  data: {\n    name: 'John Doe',\n    age: 30,\n    email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n    tags: ['tag1', 'tag2', 'tag3'],\n    address: {\n      street: '123 Main St',\n      city: 'Anytown',\n      state: 'CA',\n      zip: '12345',\n    },\n  },\n})\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003ctemplate\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.RootProvider :class=\"styles.Root\" :value=\"jsonTreeView\"\u003e\n    \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree :class=\"styles.Tree\"\u003e\n      \u003ctemplate #arrow\u003e\n        \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n      \u003c/template\u003e\n    \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.RootProvider\u003e\n\u003c/template\u003e\n\n```\n\n#### Svelte\n\n```svelte\n\u003cscript lang=\"ts\"\u003e\n  import { JsonTreeView, useJsonTreeView } from '@ark-ui/svelte/json-tree-view'\n  import { ChevronRightIcon } from 'lucide-svelte'\n  import styles from 'styles/json-tree-view.module.css'\n\n  const jsonTreeView = useJsonTreeView({\n    defaultExpandedDepth: 1,\n    data: {\n      name: 'John Doe',\n      age: 30,\n      email: 'john.doe@example.com',\n      tags: ['tag1', 'tag2', 'tag3'],\n      address: {\n        street: '123 Main St',\n        city: 'Anytown',\n        state: 'CA',\n        zip: '12345',\n      },\n    },\n  })\n\u003c/script\u003e\n\n\u003cJsonTreeView.RootProvider class={styles.Root} value={jsonTreeView}\u003e\n  \u003cJsonTreeView.Tree class={styles.Tree}\u003e\n    {#snippet arrow()}\n      \u003cChevronRightIcon /\u003e\n    {/snippet}\n  \u003c/JsonTreeView.Tree\u003e\n\u003c/JsonTreeView.RootProvider\u003e\n\n```\n\n\u003e If you're using the `RootProvider` component, you don't need to use the `Root` component.\n\n## API Reference\n\n**Component API Reference**\n\n#### React\n\n**JsonTreeViewRoot Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `canRename` | `(node: JsonNode\u003cany\u003e, indexPath: IndexPath) =\u003e boolean` | No | Function to determine if a node can be renamed |\n| `checkedValue` | `string[]` | No | The controlled checked node value |\n| `collapseStringsAfterLength` | `number` | No |  |\n| `data` | `{}` | No | The data to display in the tree. |\n| `defaultCheckedValue` | `string[]` | No | The initial checked node value when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the checked node value. |\n| `defaultExpandedDepth` | `number` | No | The default expand level. |\n| `defaultExpandedValue` | `string[]` | No | The initial expanded node ids when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the expanded node value. |\n| `defaultFocusedValue` | `string` | No | The initial focused node value when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the focused node value. |\n| `defaultSelectedValue` | `string[]` | No | The initial selected node value when rendered.\nUse when you don't need to control the selected node value. |\n| `expandedValue` | `string[]` | No | The controlled expanded node ids |\n| `expandOnClick` | `boolean` | No | Whether clicking on a branch should open it or not |\n| `focusedValue` | `string` | No | The value of the focused node |\n| `groupArraysAfterLength` | `number` | No |  |\n| `ids` | `Partial\u003c{ root: string; tree: string; label: string; node: (value: string) =\u003e string }\u003e` | No | The ids of the tree elements. Useful for composition. |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `loadChildren` | `(details: LoadChildrenDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e Promise\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e[]\u003e` | No | Function to load children for a node asynchronously.\nWhen provided, branches will wait for this promise to resolve before expanding. |\n| `maxPreviewItems` | `number` | No |  |\n| `onBeforeRename` | `(details: RenameCompleteDetails) =\u003e boolean` | No | Called before a rename is completed. Return false to prevent the rename. |\n| `onCheckedChange` | `(details: CheckedChangeDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Called when the checked value changes |\n| `onExpandedChange` | `(details: ExpandedChangeDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e void` | No | Called when the tree is opened or closed |\n| `onFocusChange` | `(details: FocusChangeDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e void` | No | Called when the focused node changes |\n| `onLoadChildrenComplete` | `(details: LoadChildrenCompleteDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e void` | No | Called when a node finishes loading children |\n| `onLoadChildrenError` | `(details: LoadChildrenErrorDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e void` | No | Called when loading children fails for one or more nodes |\n| `onRenameComplete` | `(details: RenameCompleteDetails) =\u003e void` | No | Called when a node label rename is completed |\n| `onRenameStart` | `(details: RenameStartDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e void` | No | Called when a node starts being renamed |\n| `onSelectionChange` | `(details: SelectionChangeDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e void` | No | Called when the selection changes |\n| `quotesOnKeys` | `boolean` | No | Whether to show quotes on the keys. |\n| `scrollToIndexFn` | `(details: ScrollToIndexDetails\u003cJsonNode\u003cany\u003e\u003e) =\u003e void` | No | Function to scroll to a specific index.\nUseful for virtualized tree views. |\n| `selectedValue` | `string[]` | No | The controlled selected node value |\n| `selectionMode` | `'single' | 'multiple'` | No | Whether the tree supports multiple selection\n- \"single\": only one node can be selected\n- \"multiple\": multiple nodes can be selected |\n| `showNonenumerable` | `boolean` | No |  |\n| `typeahead` | `boolean` | No | Whether the tree supports typeahead search |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**JsonTreeViewRootProvider Props:**\n\n| Prop | Type | Required | Description |\n|------|------|----------|-------------|\n| `value` | `UseJsonTreeViewReturn` | Yes |  |\n| `asChild` | `boolean` | No | Use the provided child element as the default rendered element, combining their props and behavior. |\n| `lazyMount` | `boolean` | No | Whether to enable lazy mounting |\n| `unmountOnExit` | `boolean` | No | Whether to unmount on exit. |\n\n\n**JsonTreeViewTree
